--==_Exmh_-12629179760
Content-Type: text/plain; charset=us-ascii

Hi All,

As a result of the very helpful discussions at the recent DELOS 
Ontology Harmonization workshop, Carl and I have made some more changes 
to the ABC Ontology. These include:

1. Adding Place and Time classes - which are subclasses of Entity and 
provide the range for "atTime" and "inPlace" properties

2. Changing the name of the "State" entity to "Situation" - to remove 
the assumption of causality between states and events

3. Changing the names of the "hasInput" and "hasOutput" properties to 
"precedes" and "follows" - again to remove the implication of causality

4. Adding an "isPartOf" property and making the "isSubEventOf" 
property a subproperty of it. We've also added a "contains" property 
which is the inverse of "isPartOf".

5. Changing the name of the "inState" property which associates a 
particular phase of an actuality with a state or temporal context, to 
"inContext"

6. Changing the name of the "instanceOf" property to "phaseOf" - to 
correct confusing terminology

7. Replacing the hasAgent property with "hasPresence" and 
"hasParticipant" properties. "hasPresence" associates an Agent with an 
Event with no implication of active participation. "hasParticipant" is 
a subproperty of "hasPresence" and implies active participation of the 
Agent in an Event or Action.

We still have "Actions" - because we believe that they differ from 
Events in that they are not simply sub-events but involve an agent 
doing something. Speaking for myself, I'm still uncertain whether 
Actions should or shouldn't be a subclass of Events - at the moment 
they're not.

We no longer have an explicit "hasRole" property but use subtyping on 
the "hasParticipant" property - the "participationType" which provides 
the slot for the role. I believe this is now the same as, or very 
similar to, CIDOC/CRM's approach. You can see this in the new diagrams 
in the Annexes - though how you model this using RDF was beyond us so 
we use a fuzzy unconventional approach.

We're calling this Version 3 of the ABC Ontology. Version 2 will be 
published in the DC'2001 proceedings and Version 3, which incorporates 
the changes described above will be in the Special Issue of JODI. I've 
attached the JODI Version 3 to this email.

(BTW some of the text on the arcs in the diagrams is upside down - bug 
in SmartDraw which occurs when you change the orientation from Portrait 
to Landscape - apologies for this but beyond our control if we want 
high resolution images.)

regards,
jane
